NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
M. THANGA MUTHU JOTHIKUMAR a male child born to son of V. MANI on 28-04-1987 residing at No. 9B,
Erumai Raja Agragaram Street, Thirupathiripuliyur, Cuddalore-607 002, has been living as a female after an elaborate
sexual reassignment surgery by Dr. D. SENTHAMIL SELVI, M.B.B.S., D.G.O. CHIEF CIVIL SUREGON, GOVT HEAD
QUARTERS HOSPITAL, CUDDALORE-607 002. By this I, may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be
known as M. RAJAMATHA SRI PREMALATHA DEVI.
Cuddalore,
6th April 2015.

M. THANGA MUTHU JOTHIKUMAR.
